creations-chat 2022-11-20 13:28:07 idk but my logic would be more easier to understand i guess

*Real scale* is a "thing" that is **real sized** so from my understanding the roblox avatar height techically same height as a **kid** in real life since roblox avatar is not rlly skinny neither is tall so everything in real scale would be kinda big

mean while *Ro scale* is a "thing" that is **smaller to make it fit for roblox avatar** not too large, too wide or too tall whatever so it would be smaller and fit the avatar **perfectly** bc if ro scale roblox avatar height would be equals to **adult** size so ya it gonna be small

bonus: ro scale jet is 1 block wide
